 yah match tyagaraj stadium main hona he

" unka anubhav bhale hi kitna adhik ho lekin meraa anubhav bhi kuch kam nahin

 ) nayaa saal logon ke jivan main nai ummiden lekar aata he
 In the new year many people take the important decision to get married
 shaadi ko lekar logon ke kai sapane hote hai
 Everyone takes full care of their wedding from the location of the wedding to the wedding location
 lekin jis shaks ke saath aap apana puraa jivan gujaarne kaa soch rahe hai, us vyakti se shaadi se pehle kuch sawaal jarur kar len, taaki shaadi se pehle hi ek duusare ko behatar tareeke se samaj saken
 1
 financial condishan-shaadi se pehle kai log apane partner se ye sawaal poochna chaahate hai
 But even if they want, they are not able to ask
 kyonki kai logon ko paison se sambandhi baat poochne main thodaa dar lagata he
 However, this question is complicated, but it is very important to know about the financial condition of the partner before marriage
 2
 Family Planning- Before marriage, talk about your family planning
 jab do logon main se ek vyakti ko bacchon kii jaldi hoti he, to is cheez ko shaadi se pehle hi baat kar nirnay len ki aapako kab or kitne samay ke baad bacchon ke bare main sochna he
 3
 partner kii aadaton ke bare main puuchhen-shaadi se pehle hi apane partner kii aadaton ke bare main puuchhen ki unhen kya pasand he or kya naapsand
 By doing this many of your things will be cleared in advance, so that your married life will be happy

 pehla paper subah 9

 30 baje tak yojit hoga
 The Central Board of Secondary Education (CBSE) is conducting CTET examinations in 20 languages in 104 cities of the country
 media reports ke anusaar patna or guwahati se aavedakon kii baari sankhya ke kaaran is saal assam or bihar ke rajyon main adhik shaharon ko joda gaya he

 sitate ke desh bhar main 2942 pariksha centre banaae gaye hai

 vahiin paper-ii main 427897 aavedak isamen hissaa lenge
 a total of 838381 candidates will appear in both the papers

 has gone
 in sabhi par aarope he inhone milakar desh bhar main kareeb 15 lakh logon se 25 hajaar karod rupye thage hai
 It includes about 10 thousand investors from Kanpur, Uttar Pradesh
 in niveshkon kaa 1000 karod rupe se zyada rupye is thagi main gaye hai
 Actually this fraud was done in the name of investing in real estate companies
 kedy singh or unke chah sahyogiyon par aarope he ki unhone niveshkon ko do se chaar guna rakam karne kaa jhansa dekar unase lakhon rupye thag liye or dhire-dhire yah rakam deshbhar ke 15 lakh logon se kareeb 25 hajaar karod ban gai
 In 2010, the accused opened the office of a company named Alchemist Infra Realty Limited and Alchemist Township Limited
 isaki kanpur main bhi kai shakhaaen khuli thim jiske chairman rajyasabha saansad kedy singh the

 yahi nahin niveshkon ko tamaam tareeke se chhot or paise ko doguna, teen guna karne kaa bhi laalach diya gaya

 unki rachi 'madhushaala' kii paktiyaan amitabh kai maukon par puure manoyog se sunaate hai
 Amitabh's father named him Inklab, but at the suggestion of cinematographer Sumitranandan Pant, it was named 'amitabh', which means a never-ending aura
 amitabh ne apni padhai nainital ke prasiddh sherwood college or phir dilli vishvavidhyalay ke kirodimal college se puri kii
 Amitabh's mother was associated with Teji Theater
 unhen filmon main abhinay karne kaa prastaav mila tha, jise unhone thukraa diya tha
 Teji used to encourage Amitabh to enter the acting world
 amitabh ne kolkata main ek shipping company main naukari bhi kii, lekin abhinayta banane ke liye vah naukari chhod mumbai aa gaye
 He has struggled a lot to achieve a place in the film world
 amitabh ke chote bhai ajitabh ne abhinayta kii kuch tasveeron ko khwaja ahamed abbaas ke paas bhej diya
 In those days, Abbas was making a film called 'saat Hindustani'
 unhone ek muslim yuvak kaa kirdaar nibhaane ke liye amitabh ko chun liya
 Upon the release of the film in 1969, Amitabh went to see the film with his parents at the Sheela Cinemas
 yah film nahin chali, lekin us samay kii mashhoor abhinetri minaa kumari ne amitabh kii prashansa kii thi
 Amitabh's struggle continued
 jalaal aagaa ne ek vigyaapan company kholi thi
 Jalal would take Amitabh to a small recording center in Worli and Amitabh would get fifty rupees for a one-two-minute voiceover
 varli kii city bekri main aadhi raat ke samay toote-phute biscuit aadhe daam par mil jate the
 In this way, Amitabh used to eat toast in the restaurants of the campus corner, which remained open overnight, and would go out in search of work the next morning
 abbaas sahab ke kehane par rishikesh mukherjee ne unhen film 'anand' main kaam de diya
 The film had the then superstar Rajesh Khanna in the lead role
 film safal rahi or amitabh bhi gambhir bhoomika main logon kaa dhyaan apni ore khinchne main kaamyaab rahe
 Amitabh was getting most of the side roles
 unhone phir mahmud kii film 'bambe tu goa' main kaam kiya
 His naughty style was well received by the audience
 'zanjeer' ke hit hone se pehle amitabh kii lagbhag ek darjan filmein asafal raheen
 Seeing work in the film 'bombay to Goa', Prakash Mehra and Salim Javed chose Amitabh for 'zanjeer'
 is film ko devanand or dharmedra sahit kai bade kalakaar thukraa chuke the
 The film was a tremendous hit
 amitabh ne us samay kii safal abhinetri jaya bhadudi se kaha tha ki agar film safal ho gai to donon landan jaakar iskaa jashn maanaayenge
 When father Harivansh Rai Bachchan got the idea, he said that both can go to London only by getting married
 3 june 1973 ko donon parinay sutara main bandha gaye
 Both have two children - Abhishek Bachchan and Shweta Nanda
 san 70 or 80 ke dashak main amitabh ne 'abhimaan', 'namak haraam', 'diwaar', 'shahenshaah', 'kuli', 'don', 'agnipath', 'kabhi-kabhi', 'sholay', 'kuli', jaisi shandaar filmon main kaam kiya
 The film Wall brought Amitabh to new heights of fame
 unhen bollywood main engri yangamain ke naam se pukaara jane laga
 But, Yash Chopra gave him a chance to work in romantic films
 Sometimes, he was also liked as a thrilled hero in films like Silsila etc
 'do anjaane' (1976) main pehali baar rekha or amitabh ne saath kaam kiya
 Rekha fell in love with Amitabh's acting and personality
 amitabh bhi rekha kii khubsuurati ke diwane ho gaye
 But wife Jaya shows patience and she finally manages to get Amitabh back
 film 'silsilaa' (1981) ke saath donon ke saath kaam karne kaa silsilaa bhi khatm ho gaya
 When Rekha received the National Award for 'umrao Jaan', Amitabh was the first to call Rekha and congratulate her
 san 1982 main film 'kuli' kii shooting ke dauraan ek ection drishy ko filmaate vakt sah abhinayta punit issar ke ghunse se amitabh gambhir rup se ghayal ho gaye
 He had a deep injury to his bowel
 chikitsak bhi kuch kehane kii sthiti main nahin the
 In such a situation, Jaya used to recite Hanuman Chalisa while sitting at Amitabh's head
 aspataal main jaya ne hi pehali baar amitabh kaa angootha hilte dekha or chikitsakon ko soochna di
 The whole country was blissful when Amitabh regained consciousness and recovered
 amitabh ne apane mitra rajeev gandhi kii salaah par raajnneeti main bhi kadam rakhaa tha
 In 1984, he won the Lok Sabha election defeating former Uttar Pradesh Chief Minister Hemanandan Bahuguna
 lekin, raajnneeti amitabh ko raas nahin ai or boforce top saude main apana naam uchhalane par unhone raajnneeti se sadaa ke liye kinaaraa kar liya
 Big b started a company called Amitabh Bachchan Corporation Limited (ABCL) in 1995
 1996 main abisiel ne bangaloru main vishwa sundari pratiyogita kaa aayojan kiya
 After this, the company suffered a lot of losses, Amitabh became a debtor
 unki mali haalat ladkadaa gai
 Many famous producers also distanced themselves from the actor in bad times
 aise main varsh 2000 main tivi sho 'koun banegaa karodpati' unke liye bada sahaara bana
 The show went on and Amitabh started working again
 bachchan ne 2013 main film 'da great gatsbai' se hollywood main kadam rakhaa
 Amitabh has received many accolades in recent years from many successful films like 'baghban', 'black' and 'paa'
 tippaniyan Now the stories of films are written keeping in mind a character like him
 haal hi main amitabh ko 'piku' ke liye rashtriya puraskaar se nawaja gaya
 In 2000, the actor was awarded the title of the great hero of the century
 amitabh bataur sarvshereshth abhinayta 15 baar filmphere puraskaar jeet chuke hai
 His wax figure is kept in the Madame Tussauds Museum in London
 amitabh ko 1984 main padmashri, 2001 main padmabhushan or 2015 main padmavibhushan sammaan mil chukaa he
 Amitabh Bachchan Sports Complex has been opened by the Uttar Pradesh Sports Directorate in the name of the actor
 haal hi main pradarshit film 'pink' main amitabh ke kaam ko darshakon ne khub pasand kiya he
 Big b Happy Birthday !!! (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Amitabh completed his studies at the famous Sherwood College in Nainital and then Kirori Mal College of Delhi University
 amitabh kii maa teji rangamanch se judi hui thim
 He received an offer to act in films, which he turned down
 teji amitabh ko abhinay kii duniya main jane ke liye protsaahit karti rahati thim
 Amitabh also worked in a shipping company in Kolkata, but left the job to Mumbai to become an actor
 filmi duniya main mukaam hasil karne ke liye unhone bahut sangharsh kiya he
 Amitabh's younger brother Ajitabh sent some pictures of the actor to Khwaja Ahmed Abbas
 un dinon abbaas 'saat hindustani' naam kii film bana rahe the
 He chose Amitabh to play the role of a Muslim youth
 1969 main yah film relies hone par amitabh apane mata-pita ke saath shila cinemaghar main film dekhne gaye
 The film did not go on, but Amitabh was praised by the then famous actress Meena Kumari
 amitabh kaa sangharsh jari rahaa
 Jalal Agha opened an advertising company
 jalaal amitabh ko varli ke ek chote se recordig centre le jate or ek-do minute ke woysover ke liye amitabh ko pachaas rupee mil jate the
 Broken biscuits were available at half the price at midnight in Worli's City Bakery
 amitabh is tarah kai baar raatbhar khule rahane vaale campus carnor ke restaraaon main toast khaakar guzaara karte or agali subah phir kaam kii talash main nikal jate
 At the behest of Abbas saheb, Hrishikesh Mukherjee hired him for the film 'anand'
 is film main us samay ke super star rajesh khanna mukhya bhoomika main the
 The film was a success and Amitabh also managed to grab the attention of people in a serious role
 amitabh ko adhikansh said role hi mil rahe the
 He then acted in Mahmood's film Bombay to Goa
 unke natkhat andaaj ko darshakon ne khub saraahaa
 About a dozen of Amitabh's films failed before 'zanjeer' hit
 'bambe tu goa' film main kaam dekhakar prakaash mehara or saleem javed ne amitabh ko 'zanjeer' ke liye chun liya
 The film was rejected by many big actors including Devanand and Dharmendra
 film jabardast hit rahi
 Amitabh had told then successful actress Jaya Bhaduri that if the film was successful, both would go to London to celebrate it
 jab pita harivansh raay bachchan ko isaki bhanak lagi to unhone kaha ki donon shaadi karke hi landan ja sakate hai
 On June 3, 1973, the two tied the knot
 donon kii do santan- abhishek bachchan or shweta nanda hai
 In the 70s and 80s, Amitabh played 'abhimaan', 'namak Haram', 'wall', 'emperor', 'coolie', 'don', 'agneepath', 'sometimes', 'sholay', 'coolie' ', Jesse worked in spectacular films
 diwaar film ne amitabh ko shoharat kii nai bulandiyon par pahunchaaya
 He was called as Angry Youngman in Bollywood
 lekin, yash chopra ne unhen romantic filmon main kaam karne kaa mauka diya kabhi-kabhi, silsilaa aadi filmon main unhen romantit hero ke rup main bhi darshakon ne khub pasand kiya
 Rekha and Amitabh worked together for the first time in 'do Anjaane' (1976)
 rekha shaadishuda amitabh ke abhinay or vyaktvi se prabhavit hokar unke pyaar main pad gayi
 Amitabh also became crazy about Rekha's beauty
 magar patni jaya ne dhairya kaa parichay diya or vah aakhirkaar amitabh ko waapas paane main kaamyaab raheen
 The work of the two ended with the film 'silsila' (1981)
 jab 'umrao jaan' ke liye rekha ko rashtriya puraskaar mila to sabase pehle amitabh ne rekha ko phone kar badhai di thi
 During the shooting of the film 'coolie' in 1982, Amitabh was severely injured by the punches of co-actor Puneet Issar while filming an action scene
 unki aant main gahari chot lagi thi
 The doctors were also not in a position to say anything
 aise main jaya, amitabh ke sirahaane baith hanuman chalisa kaa paath kiya karti thim
 In the hospital, Jaya saw Amitabh's thumb moving for the first time and informed the doctors
 amitabh ko hosh aane or swasth hone par puraa desh khushi se jhum uthaa tha
 Amitabh also stepped into politics on the advice of his friend Rajiv Gandhi
 1984 main unhone uttar pradesh ke purv mukhyamantri hemanandan bahuguna ko haraa loksabhaa chunaav jeeta tha
 However, politics did not go down well with Amitabh and he opted out of politics forever after his name cropped up in the Bofors gun deal
 big bi ne 1995 main amitabh bachchan corporation limited (abisiel) naam kii company shuru kii
 In 1996, ABCL organized the World Sundry Competition in Bangalore
 iske baad is company ko kaaphi nuksaan hua amitabh karjadaar ban gaye
 His financial condition faltered
 kai mashhoor nirmaataaon ne bhi bure vakt main abhinayta se kinaaraa kar liya
 So in the year 2000, the TV show 'kaun Banega Crorepati' became a big support for him
 sho chal niklaa or amitabh ko phir se kaam milane laga
 Bachchan made her Hollywood debut in 2013 with the film 'the Great Gatsby'
 amitabh ne haal ke varsho main 'bagban', 'blike' or 'paa' jaisi kai safal filmon se khub tarifbatori
 The comments ab unke jaise kirdaar ko dhyaan main rakhkar filmon kii kahaniyaan likhi jaati hai
 Recently, Amitabh was awarded the National Award for 'piku'
 2000 main abhinayta ko sadi ke mahanayake ke khitaab se nawaja gaya
 Amitabh has won the Filmfare Award 15 times as Best Actor
 unke mom kaa putala landan ke madam tusaad sangrahalay main rakhaa gaya he
 Amitabh has received Padma Shri in 1984, Padma Bhushan in 2001 and Padma Vibhushan in 2015

 Amitabh's work has been well received by the audience in the recently released film 'pink'
